2025-01-22T19:35:17Z #11 177.4 To enable CUDA support, UCX requires the CUDA Runtime library (libcudart).
2025-01-22T19:35:17Z #11 177.4 The library can be installed with the appropriate command below:
2025-01-22T19:35:17Z #11 177.4 
2025-01-22T19:35:17Z #11 177.4 * For CUDA 11, run:    conda install cudatoolkit cuda-version=11
2025-01-22T19:35:17Z #11 177.4 * For CUDA 12, run:    conda install cuda-cudart cuda-version=12
2025-01-22T19:35:17Z #11 177.4 
2025-01-22T19:35:17Z #11 177.4 
2025-01-22T19:35:17Z #11 177.4 To enable CUDA support, please follow UCX's instruction above.
2025-01-22T19:35:17Z #11 177.4 
2025-01-22T19:35:17Z #11 177.4 To additionally enable NCCL support, run:    conda install nccl
2025-01-22T19:35:17Z #11 177.4 
2025-01-22T19:35:17Z #11 177.4 
2025-01-22T19:35:17Z #11 177.4 On Linux, Open MPI is built with CUDA awareness but it is disabled by default.
2025-01-22T19:35:17Z #11 177.4 To enable it, please set the environment variable
2025-01-22T19:35:17Z #11 177.4 OMPI_MCA_opal_cuda_support=true
2025-01-22T19:35:17Z #11 177.4 before launching your MPI processes.
2025-01-22T19:35:17Z #11 177.4 Equivalently, you can set the MCA parameter in the command line:
2025-01-22T19:35:17Z #11 177.4 mpiexec --mca opal_cuda_support 1 ...
2025-01-22T19:35:17Z #11 177.4 Note that you might also need to set UCX_MEMTYPE_CACHE=n for CUDA awareness via
2025-01-22T19:35:17Z #11 177.4 UCX. Please consult UCX documentation for further details.

2025-01-22T19:39:51Z #11 451.3

2025-01-22T19:39:51Z #11 451.3 
2025-01-22T19:39:51Z #11 451.3 
2025-01-22T19:39:51Z #11 451.3 On Linux, Open MPI is built with CUDA awareness but it is disabled by default.
2025-01-22T19:39:51Z #11 451.3 To enable it, please set the environment variable
2025-01-22T19:39:51Z #11 451.3 OMPI_MCA_opal_cuda_support=true
2025-01-22T19:39:51Z #11 451.3 before launching your MPI processes.
2025-01-22T19:39:51Z #11 451.3 Equivalently, you can set the MCA parameter in the command line:
2025-01-22T19:39:51Z #11 451.3 mpiexec --mca opal_cuda_support 1 ...
2025-01-22T19:39:51Z #11 451.3 Note that you might also need to set UCX_MEMTYPE_CACHE=n for CUDA awareness via
2025-01-22T19:39:51Z #11 451.3 UCX. Please consult UCX documentation for further details.
